	<div id="helpDetailContainer" class="col-sm-9 help-detail-container">
		<div id="dragAndCopyDiv" class="help-detail-div">
			<div class="help-detail-header ">Drag And Copy</div>
			<p>1. Select the cell.</p>
			<p>2. Drag the cell-selection outline to the place where you want the copy to appear and release the mouse button.</p>
			<p>3. Press Ctrl + D.</p>
		</div>
		<div id="copyAndPasteDiv" class="help-detail-div">
			<div class="help-detail-header ">Copy And Paste</div>
			<p>1. Select single or multiple records.</p>
			<p>2. Press Ctrl + C.</p>
			<p>3. Select a row where you want single or multiple records are to be paste.</p>
			<p>4. Press Ctrl + V. All records will be pasted down starting from selected row.</p>
		</div>
		<div id="findAndReplaceDiv" class="help-detail-div">
			<div class="help-detail-header ">Find And Replace</div>
			<p>This is a column level operation. Once you select a column, you will see the option of Find and Replace.</p>
			<p>1. Select a column where you want to search the value to be replaced.</p>
			<p>2. Click Find and Replace transform.</p>
			<p>3. Enter the value you want to replace and the value you want to replace it with.</p>
		</div>
		<div id="removeRowsDiv" class="help-detail-div">
			<div class="help-detail-header ">Remove Rows</div>
			<p>This is a row level operation. Once you select row(s), you will see the option to Remove Rows.</p>
			<p>1. Select single or multiple rows</p>
			<p>2. Click on Remove Rows.</p>
			<p>3. Confirm the deletion.</p>
			<p>4. Commit changes.</p>
			<p> Note that this will permanently remove the records from your data source. </p>
		</div>
